posted:Posted April 15, 2024
msg:Lanzhou Shengda Hilton Hotel has the worst overall experience among Hilton hotels, bar none. I rarely write accommodation reviews. Mainly because everyone's accommodation experience is different, so untrue and objective reviews will lead to different understandings of the reviews. This stay experience compelled me to write a review and share it with you. It‚Äôs not specifically slanderous, nor is it slanderous. You can take a closer look. I hope it can provide some help to everyone's accommodation. I also hope that this so-called top luxury hotel can provide more customers with services that match high-end luxury hotels because of my stay experience. This is the usefulness of this comment. I will attach a picture to each question to prove the authenticity of my comments. Of course, there are some service items but there are no photos. I can only objectively restore the services.
First check into the hotel. Check-in is not on the first floor, but on the 51st floor. However, there is indeed no obvious signage in the lobby on the first floor. Only when you get near the service desk can you see a check-in sign on the 51st floor on the wall. However, when I arrived at the hotel, there was no service staff in the entire lobby. Another resident told me that the waiter had gone to get something, which meant that there was only one service staff in the entire lobby at that time. I waited here for five minutes before the front desk clerk came over and told me that I could go to the 51st floor to check in. We booked a YOYO theme room. Just think about it, if two people live in an ordinary family, why would they choose a bed with a width of 2m7. I think at least as a top luxury hotel in the world, he should have thought of at least bringing a child. I think this is the minimum. Of course we were traveling with two children. One is three years old and the other is eight years old. The height of a three-year-old child is 96mm, and the height of an eight-year-old child is 1.28m. This is the main reason why we stayed in this room. The 2m7 room is enough for us to sleep.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî
Here comes the point.
There are no children's items in the entire room. I'm talking about children's products. There are no children's toothbrushes, no children's slippers, no children's bathrobes, no children's towels, no children's pillows, no children's toiletries, no children's care products, and no children's toilets. You may not understand that there are no pillows or towels, but what I want to say is that children are light in weight, and large pillows allow children to basically sleep semi-inclined. But there are no children's toiletries. There were no children's bathrobes and slippers, so the whole child walked around the room barefoot. It is very easy to slip. Okay, everyone may say that the slip and fall was because the child was running around, and it was nothing. So in the attached picture below, please take a look at the various facilities in this room. Are there any potential dangers? I have attached pictures below. The height of the sharp corners of various copper products is exactly the same as the child's face and face. Because there are no children's toiletries, our older children use adult ones. Because the basin itself is designed to be higher than the sink, the toiletries are placed on the countertop, and the glass is poured on it during use. The basin exploded and exploded. We immediately apologized to the front desk and offered to compensate for the cup.
Lanzhou was relatively dry that day. All the windows in the hotel could not be opened and had been locked. The whole room was unbearably hot. When the air conditioner was turned on, there was no cooling. The air volume was set to the lowest level and the wind blowing out was also hot. At our request, Customer service delivered a cylindrical floor fan to us. The fan was turned on all night long and faced the wall to blow air. Even so, our family of four did not cover ourselves with quilts, but covered ourselves with large bath towels. There was an episode. At about 11 o'clock in the evening, we wanted to open the door to ventilate and cool down, only to find that the door of house 3512 is directly facing the corridor, so anyone who enters or exits the elevator has the same view of this room. There was no way we could close the door again. Two adults were bitten by mosquitoes at the same time. Height standard: Children between 1.2 meters and 1.5 meters tall need to purchase a child ticket, which is half the price of an adult ticket. Why do you need to make up the ticket?
